     <div class="row"> 
      <div class="span12"> 
       <h1 class="page-header">Federal Governmental Relations</h1> 
      </div> 
      <div class="span12"> 
       <ul class="nav nav-tabs sub-nav tab5"> 
        <li class="active"><a class="" href="index.html">Overview</a></li> 
        <li class=""><a class="" href="staff-liaisons/index.html">Staff &amp; liaisons</a></li> 
        <li class=""><a class="multiline" href="sequestration/index.html">Federal Budget &amp; Sequestration</a></li> 
        <li class=""><a class="" href="policy-legislation/index.html">Policy &amp; Legislation</a></li> 
        <li class=""><a class="" href="resources/index.html">Resources</a></li> 
       </ul> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <!-- Example row of columns --> 
     <div class="row-fluid"> 
      <div class="span4 hero-unit"> 
       <p>We are UC's liaison to the federal government.</p> 
      </div> 
      <div class="span4">
       <p>The University of California's Office of&nbsp;Federal Governmental Relations&nbsp;is located at the UC Washington Center in Washington, DC.&nbsp;<span>As the largest public research institution in the world, the university engages in numerous partnerships with federal education, health care and research agencies.&nbsp;</span>Working with Congress, the administration, federal agencies and national organizations, we advocate for the university and its missions in education, research and public service.</p>
      </div> 
      <div class="span4"> 
       <div class="row-fluid dotted-bottom"> 
        <div class="span4 dept-head"> 
         <img alt="Gary Falle" src="_files/falle.jpg" />
        </div> 
        <div class="span8"> 
         <p class="blue"> <a href="staff-liaisons/bios/gary-falle.html">Gary Falle</a> </p> 
         <p>Associate Vice President</p> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="row-fluid"> 
        <div class="span6"> 
         <a class="icon staff" href="staff-liaisons/index.html">Staff Directory</a>
        </div> 
        <div class="span6"> 
         <a class="icon org" href="_files/fgr-org-chart.pdf">Org Chart</a>
        </div> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div>

      if (spaceForContent >= SNAP_WIDTH_3) {
        return ytpreload.SnapClassList[2];
      } else if (spaceForContent >= SNAP_WIDTH_2){
        return ytpreload.SnapClassList[1];
      } else {
        return ytpreload.SnapClassList[0];
      }

    };
    ytpreload.GUIDE_PINNED_CLASS = 'guide-pinned';
    ytpreload.GUIDE_VISIBILITY_CLASS = 'show-guide';
    ytpreload.usePinnedGuideStyle = function() {
      var screenWidth = window.innerWidth ||
          document.documentElement.clientWidth;
      return screenWidth >= 1251;
    };
    (function() {
      var htmlEl = document.getElementsByTagName('html')[0];
      var classList = [htmlEl.className];
        if (ytpreload.usePinnedGuideStyle()) {
          classList.push(ytpreload.GUIDE_PINNED_CLASS);
            classList.push(ytpreload.GUIDE_VISIBILITY_CLASS);
        }
        classList.push(' ', ytpreload.getSnapClass(
            true));
      htmlEl.className = classList.join(' ');
    })();
  </script>

        // Google WaterMark Script
        $(function () {
            $("#txtGoogleSearch").each(function () {
                ToggleHint($(this)); // add class on page load to elements with "hintable" class
            });

            $("#txtGoogleSearch").focus(function () {
                $(this).removeClass("GoogleWatermark"); // handle all focus hints
            });

            $("#txtGoogleSearch").blur(function () {
                ToggleHint(this); // handle all blur hints
            });
        });

        function ToggleHint(obj) {
            if ($(obj).val() == '') { $(obj).addClass("GoogleWatermark"); };
        }

     <img src="/Images/schedule-of-classes.png" alt="" class="page-lead" /> 
     <div class="span-9"> 
      <h3 style="margin-bottom: 15px;">Design Your Perfect Schedule</h3> 
      <h4>Build Your Schedule</h4> 
      <p>Search the <a href="/registrar/schedule-of-classes/classes.aspx">Schedule of Classes</a> for class times, locations and instructors. Plan for alternatives and write down your top choices to make registration easy.</p> 
      <h4>Explore the Catalog</h4> 
      <p>Browse courses in the <a href="/registrar/schedule-of-classes/catalog.aspx">General Catalog</a>, download it to your mobile device or print it out by section. </p> 
      <h4>UC Online Courses</h4> 
      <p>In upcoming Winter/Spring 2014 terms, the University of California is launching a pilot series of online courses offered by various UC campuses. Eligible UC undergraduate students can enroll simultaneously in another UCs online course. Add/drop dates vary by campus and by the quarter/semester calendar. No additional tuition is assessed; however, other fees may apply depending on the course. Course credit is calculated in a students UC GPA. Students should meet with their adviser before enrolling to confirm course applicability toward their degree. For more information regarding available courses and registration please go to <a href="http://crossenroll.universityofcalifornia.edu">crossenroll.universityofcalifornia.edu</a>.</p> 
      <h4>See Archives</h4> 
      <p> To see the Schedule of Classes and General Catalogs from past years, please use our<a href="/registrar/archives/default.aspx"> Archives</a>.</p> 
      <p>&nbsp;</p>

  <div class="pagewrapper"> 
   <h3 class="accessibility">Footer</h3> 
   <div id="colophon">
     The University of California, Riverside (
    <a href="http://www.ucr.edu/">www.ucr.edu</a>) is a doctoral research university, a living laboratory for groundbreaking exploration of issues critical to Inland Southern California, the state and communities around the world. Reflecting California's diverse culture, UCR's enrollment has exceeded 21,000 students. The campus opened a medical school in 2013 and has reached the heart of the Coachella Valley by way of the UCR Palm Desert Center. The campus has an annual statewide economic impact of more than $1 billion. A broadcast studio with fiber cable to the AT&amp;T Hollywood hub is available for live or taped interviews. UCR also has ISDN for radio interviews. To learn more, call (951) UCR-NEWS. 
   </div>
